```python
data['市值_lag1'] = data.groupby("证券代码")['市值'].shift(1)
data['账面市值比_lag1'] = data.groupby("证券代码")['账面市值比'].shift(1)
data['ROE_lag1'] = data.groupby("证券代码")['ROE'].shift(1)
data['总资产增长率_lag1'] = data.groupby("证券代码")['总资产增长率'].shift(1)
```


```python
dates = list(data.日期.unique())
```


```python
def get_factors(date, dat):
    new = dat[dat['日期'] == date].copy()
    
    new['SB'] = new['市值_lag1'].map(lambda x: 'B' if x >= new['市值_lag1'].median() else 'S')
    
    border_down1, border_up1 = new['账面市值比_lag1'].quantile([0.3, 0.7])
    border_down2, border_up2 = new['ROE_lag1'].quantile([0.3, 0.7])
    border_down3, border_up3 = new['总资产增长率_lag1'].quantile([0.3, 0.7])
    
    new['HML'] = new['账面市值比_lag1'].map(lambda x: 'H' if x >= border_up1 else 'M')
    new['HML'] = new.apply(lambda row: 'L' if row['账面市值比_lag1'] <= border_down1 else row['HML'], axis=1)
    
    new['RMW'] = new['ROE_lag1'].map(lambda x: 'H' if x >= border_up2 else 'M')
    new['RMW'] = new.apply(lambda row: 'L' if row['ROE_lag1'] <= border_down2 else row['RMW'], axis=1)
    
    new['CMA'] = new['总资产增长率_lag1'].map(lambda x: 'H' if x >= border_up3 else 'M')
    new['CMA'] = new.apply(lambda row: 'L' if row['总资产增长率_lag1'] <= border_down3 else row['CMA'], axis=1)
    
    
    
    # 组合划分为6组
    df_HML_SL = new.query('(SB=="S") & (HML=="L")')
    df_HML_SM = new.query('(SB=="S") & (HML=="M")')
    df_HML_SH = new.query('(SB=="S") & (HML=="H")')
    df_HML_BL = new.query('(SB=="B") & (HML=="L")')
    df_HML_BM = new.query('(SB=="B") & (HML=="M")')
    df_HML_BH = new.query('(SB=="B") & (HML=="H")')
    
    # 组合划分为6组
    df_RMW_SL = new.query('(SB=="S") & (RMW=="L")')
    df_RMW_SM = new.query('(SB=="S") & (RMW=="M")')
    df_RMW_SH = new.query('(SB=="S") & (RMW=="H")')
    df_RMW_BL = new.query('(SB=="B") & (RMW=="L")')
    df_RMW_BM = new.query('(SB=="B") & (RMW=="M")')
    df_RMW_BH = new.query('(SB=="B") & (RMW=="H")')
    
    # 组合划分为6组
    df_CMA_SL = new.query('(SB=="S") & (CMA=="L")')
    df_CMA_SM = new.query('(SB=="S") & (CMA=="M")')
    df_CMA_SH = new.query('(SB=="S") & (CMA=="H")')
    df_CMA_BL = new.query('(SB=="B") & (CMA=="L")')
    df_CMA_BM = new.query('(SB=="B") & (CMA=="M")')
    df_CMA_BH = new.query('(SB=="B") & (CMA=="H")')
    
    return [
        df_HML_SL['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_HML_SM['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_HML_SH['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_HML_BL['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_HML_BM['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_HML_BH['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_RMW_SL['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_RMW_SM['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_RMW_SH['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_RMW_BL['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_RMW_BM['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_RMW_BH['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_CMA_SL['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_CMA_SM['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_CMA_SH['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_CMA_BL['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_CMA_BM['收益率'].mean(), 
        df_CMA_BH['收益率'].mean(), 
    ]

```


```python
results = []

for d in dates:
    results.append([d, *get_factors(d, data)])
    print(d)
```

## 导入上次的数据


```python
# 用上次的五因子数据和因子收益率数据
factor_df = pd.read_excel("上次数据/五因子数据.xlsx")
factor_df = factor_df.rename(columns={"时间" : "日期"})

factor_mut = pd.read_excel("上次数据/因子收益率.xlsx")
```

## 分别对每一个资产做回归


```python
import statsmodels.api as sm

def get_OLS(X, y):
    X = sm.add_constant(X)
    mod = sm.OLS(y, X)
    res = mod.fit()
    return res
```


```python
ai_list = []
ai_t_values_list = []
resid_df = pd.DataFrame()
```


```python
target_cols = ["HML_SL", "HML_SM", "HML_SH", "HML_BL", "HML_BM", "HML_BH", "RMW_SL", "RMW_SM", "RMW_SH", "RMW_BL",
"RMW_BM", "RMW_BH", "CMA_SL", "CMA_SM", "CMA_SH", "CMA_BL", "CMA_BM", "CMA_BH",]
```

# 模型一


```python
for col in target_cols:
    _ = df_res[['日期', col]].reset_index().merge(factor_df, on='日期', how='left').dropna()
    X = _[['SMB', 'HML', 'CMA', 'RMW', 'mk_rf']]
    y = _[col]
    
    res = get_OLS(X, y)
    print("异象的拟合方程：", col)
    print(res.summary())
    print("\n\n")
    
    const = res.params.loc['const']
    const_t_values = res.tvalues.loc['const']
    
    ai_list.append(['模型1', col, const])
    ai_t_values_list.append(['模型1', col, const_t_values])
    resid_df[f'模型1_{col}'] = res.resid
```

# 模型二


```python
X_cols = ['市值因子收益率', '账面市值比因子收益率', 'ROE因子收益率', '总资产增长率因子收益率']
```


```python
for col in target_cols:
    _ = df_res[['日期', col]].reset_index().merge(factor_mut, on='日期', how='left').dropna()
    
    X = _[X_cols]
    y = _[col] - _['const']

    res = get_OLS(X, y)
    print("异象的拟合方程：", col)
    print(res.summary())
    print("\n\n")
    
    const = res.params.loc['const']
    const_t_values = res.tvalues.loc['const']
    
    ai_list.append(['模型2', col, const])
    ai_t_values_list.append(['模型2', col, const_t_values])
    resid_df[f'模型2_{col}'] = res.resid
```

# 模型三


```python
X_cols_03 = ['mk_rf', '市值因子收益率', '账面市值比因子收益率', 'ROE因子收益率', '总资产增长率因子收益率']
```


```python
for col in target_cols:
    _ = df_res[['日期', col]].reset_index().merge(factor_mut, on='日期', how='left').merge(factor_df, on='日期', how='left').dropna()
    
    X = _[X_cols_03]
    y = _[col]
    
    res = get_OLS(X, y)
    print("异象的拟合方程：", col)
    print(res.summary())
    print("\n\n")
    
    const = res.params.loc['const']
    const_t_values = res.tvalues.loc['const']
    
    ai_list.append(['模型3', col, const])
    ai_t_values_list.append(['模型3', col, const_t_values])
    resid_df[f'模型3_{col}'] = res.resid
```

# GRS 检验

```python
from grs import GRS_test
```

## 模型1 GRS检验


```python
factor01 = factor_df.iloc[:, 1:].values
resid01 = resid_df[['模型1_HML_SL', '模型1_HML_SM', '模型1_HML_SH', '模型1_HML_BL', '模型1_HML_BM',
       '模型1_HML_BH', '模型1_RMW_SL', '模型1_RMW_SM', '模型1_RMW_SH', '模型1_RMW_BL',
       '模型1_RMW_BM', '模型1_RMW_BH', '模型1_CMA_SL', '模型1_CMA_SM', '模型1_CMA_SH',
       '模型1_CMA_BL', '模型1_CMA_BM', '模型1_CMA_BH']].values
alpha01 = ai_df[ai_df.模型号 == '模型1'].const.values
```


```python
GRS_test(factor01, resid01, alpha01)
```




    (18.44058547756932, 1.1102230246251565e-16)
